<h2 class="city">Mochammad Rafli Eka Setyawan</h2>
<center><img class="nia12y4vjec18hc91u4912bci" src="https://pps.whatsapp.net/v/t61.24694-24/299618167_970566127674501_7286278628103720656_n.jpg?ccb=11-4&oh=01_AVxbq9uCXvRkE26XOLFMHLAPpNMDJaa-w5uru9KEs9QETw&oe=63336E0C" 
alt="Foto Profil Miliknya" width="300" height="300"></center>
<p class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Mochammad Rafli Eka Setyawan atau yang dikenal dengan penghianat legendaris, lahir pada tanggal 28 April 2007.<br>
Ia dikenal dengan panggilan penghianat legendaris karena sering menghianati teman-temannya, dan tidak merasa menyesal sekali pun.<br>
Meskipun ia terkadang jahat bukan berarti dia tidak pernah melakukan hal baik meskipun kemungkinannya terlalu kecil</p>
<p class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Ia pernah memenangkan Juara 3 Lomba Sholawat Peringatan Maulid Nabi Muhammad S.A.W 1442 H, pada tanggal 6 November 2020 atau 97 minggu yang lalu.<br>
Ia memiliki beberapa alergi, antara lain sebagai berikut:
<ul>
<li class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Alergi makan di meja</li>
<li class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Alergi berkata jujur</li>
<li class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Alergi membantu teman</li>
<li class="k10b7G71gja7hajf8na9absB">Alergi kerja kelompok</li>
</ul><br>

</p>

<H1>Kamisato Ayaka</H1>
<center><img src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/gensin-impact
/images/3/34/Character_Kamisato_Ayaka_Card.png/revision
/latest?cb=20210607100828" alt="Ayaka Picture" width="200" ></center>
<p>
<strong >Kamisato Ayaka</strong> is a playable Cryo character in Genshin Impact.
She is the oldest daughter of the Kamisato Clan and younger sister 
of Kamisato Ayato. Being beautiful, elegant, and graceful, 
the common folk have nothing to bad-mouth Ayaka about.
Because of her social status as the eldest daughter of the Kamisato
Clan of the Yashiro Commission and as the Shirasagi Himegimi, 
Ayaka is seen as a model of perfection.
</p>
<a href="https://genshin-impact.fandom.com/wiki/Kamisato_Ayaka">Kamisato Ayaka</a>

<H1>Kamisato Ayaka</H1>
<center><img class="Border" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/gensin-impact
/images/3/34/Character_Kamisato_Ayaka_Card.png/revision

<p>
<p><a href="https://genshin-impact.fandom.com/wiki/Kamisato_Ayaka"><b>Kamisato Ayaka</b></a> is a playable Cryo character in Genshin Impact.
She is the oldest daughter of the Kamisato Clan and younger sister 
of Kamisato Ayato. Being beautiful, elegant, and graceful, 
the common folk have nothing to bad-mouth Ayaka about.
Because of her social status as the eldest daughter of the Kamisato
Clan of the Yashiro Commission and as the Shirasagi Himegimi, 
Ayaka is seen as a model of perfection.</p>

<H1>Kamisato Ayaka</H1>
<center><img class="Border" src="https://c.tenor.com/12CF2zwIRP8AAAAd/ayaka.gif" alt="Ayaka Picture" width="200"></center>
<p><a href="https://genshin-impact.fandom.com/wiki/Kamisato_Ayaka"><b>Kamisato Ayaka</b></a> is a playable Cryo character in Genshin Impact.
She is the oldest daughter of the Kamisato Clan and younger sister 
of Kamisato Ayato. Being beautiful, elegant, and graceful, 
the common folk have nothing to bad-mouth Ayaka about.
Because of her social status as the eldest daughter of the Kamisato
Clan of the Yashiro Commission and as the Shirasagi Himegimi, 
Ayaka is seen as a model of perfection.</p>

    <h1 style="margin-left:10px"class="Judul">Backstory</h1>
    <p class="MainText"><b>Bagus Kun</b> dan <b>Kizons</b> bersekolah di Doktrin Kemampuan Elite, semua muridnya berisikan dengan murid-murid berbakat elite, Namun murid-murid wajib merahasiakan kemampuan mereka sendiri-sendiri.<br>Bagus Kun dan Kizons berada di kelas yang sama, mereka berdua pendiam di kelas.<br><br>
   Bagus kun selalu dikerumuni oleh cewek-cewek, dan semua orang iri kepada nya. Kizons tidak peduli dengan hal cinta karena dia adalah <b>MC</b>. Pada suatu saat Kizons menangkap basah Bagus Kun yang sedang memakai kemampuan rahasianya yaitu <b>Memanipulasi pikiran benda hidup.</b><br> Bagus Kun menjadi panik dan rela melakukan apa saja demi menyembunyikan kemampuannya, Kizons menerima permintaan tersebut.<br> Esoknya, Kizons menyuruh Bagus Kun untuk memanipulasi pikiran Guru untuk memberikan kunci jawaban ujian, dan Bagus kun lakukan. Namun Guru tersebut tidak memberikan kunci jawaban ujian sesuai perintah Bagus Kun. Bagus kun pun heran, <b>"Mengapa guru tersebut tidak menuruti perintah nya?" </b>tanya Bagus kun. <br>Bagus Kun sangat panik karena jika ia tidak bisa memanipulasi Gurunya maka kemampuan rahasia nya akan tersebar. Sampai akhirnya Bagus Kun tidak berhasil memanipulasi Gurunya, pada saat itu juga terdapat suara misterius yg menyebar kemampuan Bagus Kun. Bagus Kun bahkan tidak tau itu suara siapa.  </p>
<br>

01/04/23, 9:22â€¯pm - Ken: let submit = true;

function bekerjaFunction() {
  let jawaban = "-";
  const jawabanNama = document.getElementById("jawabanNama");
  let usia = document.getElementById("umurPacar").value;
  let pacar = document.getElementById("namaPacar").value;
  let sifat = document.getElementById("sifatPacar").value;
  const batasUsia = 18;
  const umurLoli = 12;
  let pacarShenhe = false;
  let umurHalal = false;
  let umurHaram = false;
  let umurAnak = false;

  if (pacar.length > 10) {
    alert("Nama Pacar tidak bisa lebih dari 10 huruf!");
    submit = false;
  } else if (pacar.length < 1) {
    alert("Nama Pacar harus diisi terlebih dahulu!");
    submit = false;
  } else if (sifat.length < 1) {
    alert("Kamu harus mengisi Sifat Pacarmu terlebih dahulu!");
    submit = false;
  } else if (usia == null) {
    alert("Kamu harus mengisi Usia Pacarmu terlebih dahulu!");
    submit = false;
  } else if (usia > "100") {
  alert("Kamu tidak dapat mengisi Usia Pacar lebih dari 100 tahun, soalnya tidak logika");
  submit = false;
  
  }else {
    submit = true;
  }

  if (pacar == "Shenhe") {
    pacarShenhe = true;
  } else {
    pacarShenhe = false;
  }

  if (usia > batasUsia) {
    umurHalal = true;
  }
  if (usia == "18") {
    umurHalal = true;
  }

  if (usia < umurLoli) {
    umurAnak = true;
  }

  if (usia == "12") {
    umurAnak = true;
  }

  if (usia < batasUsia) {
    umurHaram = true;
  }
  if (submit == true) {
    if (pacarShenhe == false) {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML = `Ohh, jadi nama pacarmu itu ${pacar} ya! <br>Sungguh nama yang bagus, aku menyukainya!`;
    } else {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        "Wahh, nama pacarmu sama seperti nama pacar pembuatku!<br>Benar-benar kebetulan hahaha!";
    }
    if (umurHalal == true) {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Umur pacarmu itu ${usia} tahun ya!<br>Pacarmu seharusnya sudah boleh dinikahin!<br>Ayo cepat nikahin pacarmu sebelum diambil sama yang lain!`;
    } else if (umurAnak == true) {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Waduh, pacar kamu masih umur segitu?<br>Ini boongan kan?<br>Kamu ini sedang boongin aku kan?`;
    } else if (umurHaram == true) {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Kamu belum boleh menikahi pacarmu yaa!<br>Kamu harus menunggu ${
          batasUsia - usia
        } tahun lagi agar pacarmu mencapai Umur 18 tahun.`;
    }
    if (sifat == "Baik") {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Beruntung banget kamu dapet pacar yang baik!<br>Apa semua pacar itu baik ya?<br>Aku jadi pingin dapet pacar juga, meskipun itu mustahil karena aku hanyalah tulisan :(`;
    } else if (sifat == "baik") {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Beruntung banget kamu dapet pacar yang baik!<br>Apa semua pacar itu baik ya?<br>Aku jadi pingin dapet pacar juga, meskipun itu mustahil karena aku hanyalah tulisan :(`;
    } else if (sifat == "jahat") {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Jika Pacarmu jahat pasti ada alasannya.<br>Coba kamu pahami lebih baik dan juga sayangi dia lebih banyak!`;
    } else if (sifat == "Jahat") {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Jika Pacarmu jahat pasti ada alasannya.<br>Coba kamu pahami lebih baik dan juga sayangi dia lebih banyak!`;
    } else {
      jawabanNama.innerHTML =
        jawabanNama.innerHTML +
        `<br><br>Maaf sifat yang kamu berikan belum ada di dalam data ku.<br>Pembuatku akan segera menambahkannya ke dalam data ku, Maaf yaa!`;
    }
  }
}

07/08/23, 5:13â€¯pm - Bagus Smp: **[NEW PRIVATE SERVER COMMAND]**
- /serverlock
mengunci server agar orang tidak bisa masuk / join ( Hanya Server Owner Yang Bisa lakukan ini )

- /serverunlock
membuka server yang sudah terkunci ( Hanya Server Owner Yang Bisa lakukan ini )

- /shutdown
menshutdown server agar semua player terkick dari server ( Hanya Server Owner Yang Bisa lakukan ini )

- /moderator {playername} --// Contoh ( /moderator DA0ZA )
memberi orang Akses untuk ban, kick, dan message ( Hanya Server Owner Yang Bisa lakukan ini )

- /unmoderator {playername} --// Contoh ( /unmoderator DA0ZA )
melepas akses moderator seseorang ( Hanya Server Owner Yang Bisa lakukan ini )

- /message {message} --// Contoh ( /message Car meet di bsd ya )
memberi pesan kesetiap player di server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /time {number} --// Contoh ( /time 10, /time 16 )
mengatur waktu di server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /freezetime
memberhentikan waktu di server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /unfreezetime
menjalankan kembali waktu di server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /fog {number} --// Contoh ( /fog 0.5 )
menambahkan kabut di server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /kick {playername} --// Contoh ( /kick DA0ZA )
kick orang dari server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /ban {playername} --// Contoh ( /ban DA0ZA )
banned orang dari server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

- /unban {playername} --// Contoh ( /unban DA0ZA )
unbanned orang dari server ( Moderator dan Server Owner Bisa Melakukan Ini )

   do {

    int programNum = (rand() % 3) + 1;
    int playerNum = 0, whileValue = 0;
    string playerString;

    cout << endl;
    
    cout << "==== Rock Paper Scissors Game ===="  <<endl;

    do {
        if (!whileValue) {
            whileValue += 1;
            cout << "Choose one (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
            getline(cin, playerString);
        } else {
            cout << "Choose one first (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
            getline(cin, playerString);
        }
    } while(playerString.empty());
    do {
        if (playerString == "rock" || playerString == "Rock"){
        playerNum = 1;
    } else if (playerString == "paper" || playerString == "Paper"){
        playerNum = 2;
    } else if (playerString == "scissors" || playerString == "Scissors"){
        playerNum = 3;
    } else {
        cout << "Please only choose between (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
        getline(cin, playerString);
    }
    }while(!playerNum);
    cout << endl;

    cout << "==================================" <<endl;
    /*
    Rock = 1
    Paper = 2
    Scissors = 3
    */
    if

    (playerNum == 1 && programNum == 1) {
        cout << "Its a draw !" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Rock and so did you!" << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 1 && programNum == 2) {
        cout << "You lose :(" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Paper and you are Rock." << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 1 && programNum == 3) {
        cout << "You win !!" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Scissors and you are Rock!" << endl;
    }
    
    // Paper
    
    else if (playerNum == 2 && programNum == 1) {
        cout << "You win !!" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Rock and you are Paper!" << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 2 && programNum == 2) {
        cout << "Its a draw !" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Paper and so did you!" << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 2 && programNum == 3) {
        cout << "You lose :(" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Scissors and you are Paper." << endl;
    }

    // Scissors

    else if (playerNum == 3 && programNum == 1) {
        cout << "You lose :(" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Rock and you are Scissors." << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 3 && programNum == 2) {
        cout << "You win !!" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose Paper and you are Scissors!" << endl;
    } else if (playerNum == 3 && programNum == 3) {
        cout << "Its a draw !" << endl;

string playerInput(string playerString){
    bool whileValue = false;
    do {
        if (!whileValue) {
            whileValue = true;
            cout << "Choose one (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
            getline(cin, playerString);
        } else {
            cout << "Choose one first (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
            getline(cin, playerString);
        }
    } while(playerString.empty());

    return playerString;
}


int playerGuess(int num, string playerString){
    do {
        if (playerString == "rock" || playerString == "Rock"){
        num = 1;
    } else if (playerString == "paper" || playerString == "Paper"){
        num = 2;
    } else if (playerString == "scissors" || playerString == "Scissors"){
        num = 3;
    } else {
        cout << "Please only choose between (Rock, Paper, Scissors) : ";
        getline(cin, playerString);
    }
    }while(!num);

    return num;
}


string programGuesser(int num){
    string choice;
    do {
        if (num == 1){
         choice = "Rock";
            
        } else if (num == 2){
        choice = "Paper";
            
        } else if (num == 3){
        choice == "Rock";

        } else {
        cout << "ERROR" << endl;
        }
    } while(choice.empty());

    return choice;
}

string playerChoices(int num, string choice){
    do {
        if (num == 1){
         choice = "Rock";
            
        } else if (num == 2){
        choice = "Paper";
            
        } else if (num == 3){
        choice == "Rock";

        } else {
        cout << "ERROR" << endl;
        }
    } while(choice.empty());

    return choice;
}

char gameCalculate(int prChoice, int plChoice){

    char result;
    if

    //Rock
    
    (plChoice == 1 && prChoice == 1) {
        result = 'D';
    } else if (plChoice == 1 && prChoice == 2) {
        result = 'L';
    } else if (plChoice == 1 && prChoice == 3) {
        result = 'W';
    }

    //Paper

     else if (plChoice == 2 && prChoice == 1) {
        result = 'W';
    } else if (plChoice == 2 && prChoice == 2) {
        result = 'D';
    } else if (plChoice == 2 && prChoice == 3) {
        result = 'L';
    }

    //Scissors

    else if (plChoice== 3 && prChoice == 1) {
        result = 'L';
    } else if (plChoice == 3 && prChoice == 2) {
        result = 'W';
    } else if (plChoice == 3 && prChoice == 3) {
        result = 'D';
    }

    return result;
}

 void gameResult(char res, string plString, string prString){
    if (res == 'W'){
        cout << "You win !!" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose " << prString << " and you are " << plString << endl;
    } else if (res == 'L'){
        cout << "You lose :(" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose " << prString << " and you are " << plString << endl;
    } else if (res == 'D'){
        cout << "Its a draw !" << endl;
        cout << "Because the program chose " << prString << " and you are so did you!"<< endl;
    }
}

string replayChoice(string rep){
    cout << "============ REPLAY ? ============" << endl;
    cout << "Type (Y / N) : ";
    getline(cin, rep);
    return rep;
}

    do {
        if (stringChoice == "1" || stringChoice == "one" || stringChoice == "One"){
            stringChoice = " ";
            success = true;
            openAtm();

        } else if (stringChoice == "2" || stringChoice == "two" || stringChoice == "Two"){
            stringChoice = " ";
            success = true;

            cout << "1. Check bank" << endl;
            cout << "2. Work" << endl << endl;

            getline(cin, stringChoice);

        }
    }while(!success);
}

    cout << "3. Withdraw Money" << endl;

    getline(cin, stringChoice);

    bool success = 0;
    do {
        if (stringChoice == "1" || stringChoice == "one" || stringChoice == "One"){
            stringChoice = " ";
            success = true;
            showBalance(); 

        } else if (stringChoice == "2" || stringChoice == "two" || stringChoice == "Two"){
            stringChoice = " ";
            success = true;
            depositMoney();

        } else if (stringChoice == "3" || stringChoice == "three" || stringChoice == "Three"){
            stringChoice = " ";
            success = true;
            withdrawMoney();

        } else if (stringChoice == "4" || stringChoice == "four" || stringChoice == "Four"){
            stringChoice = " ";

            cout << endl;

            cout << "2. Deposit Money" << endl;
            cout << "3. Withdraw Money" << endl;
            cout << "4. Exit" << endl << endl;
            cout << "Enter your number again of the choice above : ";
            getline(cin, stringChoice);

        }
    }while(!success);
}

void startWork(){
    bool replay = false;
    do {
        srand(time(NULL));
        int programChoice = (rand() % 10) + 1;

                loop = false;

        }
       } while (loop);
    } while (replay);
}

//MENU
void menu(double Balance, double Cash){
    int Choice = 0;
    cout << endl;
    cout << "===== Life Cycle Game =====" << endl << endl;
    cout << "Your Cash right now are : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Cash << endl;
    cout << "Pick a choice : " << endl;
    cout << "1. Check bank" << endl;
    cout << "2. Work" << endl << endl;
    cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
    cin >> Choice;
    cin.clear();
    fflush(stdin);

    bool success = false;

    do {
        switch (Choice){
        case 1:
            success = true;
            openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            break;
        
        case 2:
            success = true;
            workMenu(Balance, Cash);
            break;

        default:

void depositMoney(double Balance, double Cash){
    int Choice = 0;
    double Amount = 0;
    string yesno = " ";
    atmText();
    cout << "Type 1 to Exit." << endl;
    cout << "Enter the amount to Deposit your money : $";
    cin >> Amount;
    cin.clear();
    fflush(stdin);

    bool success = false;

    do{
        if (Amount == 1) {
            openAtm(Balance, Cash);
        } else if (Amount <= 0){
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            cout << "You cant Deposit a money that below 0." << endl;
            cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
            cout << "1. Back" << endl;
            cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
            cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
            cin >> Choice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);

            if (Choice == 1){
                depositMoney(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        } else if (Cash < Amount){
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            cout << "You cant Deposit a money that bigger than your Balance." << endl;
            cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
            cout << "1. Back" << endl;
            cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
            cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
            cin >> Choice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);

            if (Choice == 1){
                depositMoney(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        }else {
            success = true;
            Choice = 0;
            cout << endl;
            cout << "Are you sure want to Deposit $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Amount << " Cash to Balance? (Y/N) : ";
            getline(cin, yesno);

            if (yesno == "y" || yesno == "Y"){
                int divided = Amount * 0.1;
                Cash -= Amount;
                Balance += Amount - divided;
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Deposit $"<< Amount <<" are successfull! :D" << endl;
                    cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Cash << endl;
                    openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Deposit $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Amount <<" are cancelled :(" << endl;
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        }
    }while(!success);
}

void withdrawMoney(double Balance, double Cash){
    int Choice = 0;
    double Amount = 0;
    string yesno = " ";
    atmText();
    cout << "Enter the amount to Withdraw your money : $";
    cin >> Amount;
    cin.clear();
    fflush(stdin);

    bool success = false;

    do{
        if (Amount == 1) {
            openAtm(Balance, Cash);
        } else if (Amount <= 0){
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            cout << "You cant Withdraw a money that below 0." << endl;
            cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
            cout << "1. Back" << endl;
            cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
            cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
            cin >> Choice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);

            if (Choice == 1){
                withdrawMoney(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        }else if (Balance < Amount) {
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            cout << "You cant Withdraw a money that bigger than your Balance." << endl;
            cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
            cout << "1. Back" << endl;
            cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
            cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
            cin >> Choice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);

            if (Choice == 1){
                withdrawMoney(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        } else {
            success = true;
            Choice = 0;
            cout << endl;
            cout << "Are you sure want to Withdraw $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Amount << " Balance to Cash? (Y/N) : ";
            getline(cin, yesno);

            if (yesno == "y" || yesno == "Y"){
                Cash = Cash + Amount;
                Balance -= Amount;
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Withdraw $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Amount <<" are successfull! :D" << endl;
                    cout << "Your Cash now is : " << Cash << endl;
                    openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Withdraw $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Amount <<" are cancelled :(" << endl;
                openAtm(Balance, Cash);
            }
        }
    }while(!success);
}

void startChaos(double Balance, double Cash){
    bool Replay = false;
    do{
        srand(time(NULL));
        int ProgramChoice = (rand() % 10) + 1;
        string Question, Answer, Choice;
        Replay = false;
        chaosText();

        if (ProgramChoice == 1){
            Question = "The mesmerizing dance of fireflies illuminated the tranquil night.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 2){
            Question = "As the aroma of freshly baked bread wafted through the cozy kitchen.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 3){
            Question = "Lost in the pages of an old, dusty book.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 4){
            Question = "The laughter of children playing in the park echoed through the crisp autumn air.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 5){
            Question = "The mysterious antique shop on the corner held an array of peculiar trinkets.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 6){
            Question = "With a steaming cup of coffee in hand, I watched the sunrise paint.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 7){
            Question = "The symphony of raindrops tapping on the windowpane provided a soothing backdrop.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 8){
            Question = "Beneath the vast canopy of stars, we laid on the grass, sharing stories and dreams.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 9){
            Question = "In the bustling city, I stumbled upon a hidden garden, a verdant oasis of serenity.";
        } else if (ProgramChoice == 10){
            Question = "Are oranges named oranges because oranges are orange or is orange named orange because oranges are orange.";
        }

        bool Loop = false;

        do{
            cout << endl;
            cout << "Type this sentences : " << Question << endl;
            cout << "Or type 1 to Exit." << endl;
            cout << "Enter : ";
            getline(cin, Answer);
            Loop = true;

            if (Answer == Question){
                Cash += 10;
                cout << endl;
                cout << "PERFECTLY CORRECT!" << endl;
                cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Cash << endl;
                cout << "Wanna work again? (Y/N) : ";
                getline(cin, Choice);

                if (Choice == "y" || Choice == "Y" || Choice == "yes" || Choice == "Yes"){
                    Replay = true;
                    Loop = false;
                } else {
                    cout << endl;
                    cout << "Work is done now, I can relax on bed and watching some CoryXKenshin.";
                    workMenu(Balance, Cash);
                    Loop = false;
            }
            } else if(Answer == "1"){
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Work cancelled, Boss are not happy about this.." << endl;
                cout << endl;
                Loop = false;
                workMenu(Balance, Cash);
            } else {
                cout << endl;
                cout << "Try again." << endl;
                cout << "Type this sentences : " << Question << endl;
                cout << "Or type 1 to Exit." << endl;
                cout << "Enter : ";
                getline(cin, Answer);
            }
        }while(Loop);
    } while(Replay);
    
}

    return Opponents[ProgramChoice];
}


void startNumFight(double Balance, double Cash){

                casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);

                fflush(stdin);

                    startNumFight(Balance, Cash);
                } else {
                    casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                }
                

            } else if (Amount < 50){
                cout << endl;
                cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
                cout << "You cant Bet a money that below $50.00" << endl;
                cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
                cout << "1. Back" << endl;
                cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
                cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";

                cin.clear();
                fflush(stdin);

                    startNumFight(Balance, Cash);
                } else {
                    casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                }

            } else if (Amount > 1000){
                cout << endl;
                cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
                cout << "You cant Bet a money that bigger than $1000.00" << endl;
                cout << "Pick a Choice : " << endl;
                cout << "1. Back" << endl;
                cout << "2. Exit" << endl;
                cout << "Enter your number of the choice above : ";
                cin >> Choice;
                cin.clear();
                fflush(stdin);

                if (Choice == 1){
                    startNumFight(Balance, Cash);
                } else {
                    casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                }
            } else {
                success = true;
                Choice = 0;
                cout << "Are you sure want to continue playing with $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Amount << "? (Y/N) : ";

                if (yesno == "y" || yesno == "Y"){
                    cout << endl;
                    cout << "======== Game Start ========" << endl << endl;

                    Sleep(5000);
                    cout << "Opponents found!" << endl;

                    Sleep(1000);
                    rerollNumFight(Balance, Cash, Amount, Opponents, Replay);
                } else {
                    casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                }
            }
        }while(!success);
    }while(Replay);
}

void rerollNumFight(double Balance, double Cash, double Amount, string Opponents, bool Replay){
    string Choice = " ";

    int ProgramChoice = (rand() % 36) + 1, PlayerChoice = (rand() % 36) + 1;
    cout << Opponents << " rolled the Number..." << endl;
    Sleep(3000);
    cout << Opponents << " rolled the Number " << ProgramChoice << "." << endl;
    Sleep(1000);
    cout << "Your turn : ";
    cin.ignore();
    cout << "You rolled the Number..." << endl;
    Sleep(3000);
    cout << "You got the Number " << PlayerChoice << "." << endl << endl;
    cout << "============================" << endl << endl;

    Sleep(1000);
    if (ProgramChoice > PlayerChoice){
        Cash -= Amount;
        cout << "You Lose!" << endl;
        cout << "A winner come from a losers who doesnt give up!" << endl;
        cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";
    } else if (ProgramChoice < PlayerChoice){
        Cash += Amount;
        cout << "You Win!" << endl;
        cout << "Dont stop until you are bored of moneys!" << endl;
        cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";
    } else {
        cout << "Its a tie!" << endl;
        cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl << endl;
        Sleep(2000);
        rerollNumFight(Balance, Cash, Amount, Opponents, Replay);       
    }

    Sleep(2000);
    cout << endl << endl;
    cout << "Wanna continue playing? (Y/N) : ";
    cin >> Choice;
    if (Choice == "Y" || Choice == "y"){
        cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl;
        Sleep(2000);
        startNumFight(Balance, Cash);
    } else {
        casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
    }
        
}

string guessNumHint(){
    srand(time(NULL));
    int ProgramChoice = (rand() % 5) + 1;
    string Hints[] = {"The number its beetwen 1-10.", "The number its between 1-10.", "The number is majestic.", "Can be divided by 1.", "A number.", "I dont have a idea."};

    return Hints[ProgramChoice];
}

void guessNumProgressingAnswer(double Balance, double Cash ,int ProgramChoice, int Amount, int Tries, bool Finish){
    string Hint = guessNumHint();
    int playerGuess = 0, Choice = 0;
        cout << "Hint : " << Hint << endl;
        cout << "You got " << Tries << " tries left." << endl;
        cout << "Enter your guess : ";
        cin >> playerGuess;
        cin.clear();
        fflush(stdin);

        bool sukses = 0;
        do{
            if (playerGuess <= 0){
                cout << endl;
                cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
                cout << "You cant guess a number below 0." << endl;
                Sleep(1000);
                cout << "Enter your guess : ";
                cin >> playerGuess;
                cin.clear();
                fflush(stdin);
            } else if (playerGuess > 10){
                cout << endl;
                cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
                cout << "You cant guess a number bigger than 10." << endl;
                Sleep(1000);
                cout << "Enter your guess : ";
                cin >> playerGuess;
                cin.clear();
                fflush(stdin);
            } else {
                sukses = true;
            }
        }while(!sukses);

        if (playerGuess != ProgramChoice){
            cout << endl;
            cout << "Progressing answer..." << endl;
            Sleep(3000);
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            if (Tries != 1){
                Tries -= 1;
                cout << "WRONG!" << endl;
                guessNumProgressingAnswer(Balance, Cash, ProgramChoice, Amount, Tries, Finish);
            } else {
                Finish = true;
                Cash -= Amount;
                cout << endl;
                cout << "YOU LOSE THE GAME!" << endl;
                cout << "The Program has choosen the number : " << ProgramChoice << endl;
                cout << "Your Cash now is $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Cash << "." << endl;
                Sleep(2000);
                cout << "Pick a choice : " << endl ;
                cout << "1. Play again" << endl ;
                cout << "2. Exit" << endl ;
                cout << "Enter your choice : ";
                cin >> Choice;
                cin.clear();
                fflush(stdin);

                switch (Choice){
                    case 1:
                        startGuessNum(Balance, Cash);
                        break;
                    case 2:
                        casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                        break;
                    default:
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            Cash += Amount;
            cout << "Progressing answer..." << endl;
            Sleep(3000);
            cout << endl;
            cout << "============================" << endl << endl;
            cout << "PERFECTLY RIGHT!" << endl;
            cout << "The Program has choosen the number : " << ProgramChoice << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is $" << setprecision(2) << fixed << Cash << "." << endl;
            Sleep(2000);
            cout << "Pick a choice : " << endl ;
            cout << "1. Play again" << endl ;
            cout << "2. Exit" << endl ;
            cout << "Enter your choice : ";
            cin >> Choice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);

            switch (Choice){
                case 1:
                    startGuessNum(Balance, Cash);
                    break;
                case 2:
                    casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
                    break;
                default:
                break;
            }
        }

}

void rpsProgramAnswer(double Balance, double Cash, double Amount){
    int ProgramChoice = (rand() % 3) + 1;
    string stringPlayerChoice = " ", stringProgramChoice = rpsProgramChoiceToString(ProgramChoice), Choice;
    cout << "Choose between Rock, Paper, Scissors." << endl;
    cout << "Type R for Rock." << endl;
    cout << "Type P for Paper." << endl;
    cout << "Type S for Scissors." << endl;
    Sleep(500);
    cout << "Enter your choice : ";
    cin >> stringPlayerChoice;
    cin.clear();
    fflush(stdin);

    cout << endl;
    cout << "Progressing Answer..." << endl;
    Sleep(2000);
    cout << endl;
    bool success = 0;
    do {
        if (stringPlayerChoice == "r" || stringPlayerChoice == "R"){
            stringPlayerChoice = "Rock";
            success = true;
        } else if (stringPlayerChoice == "p" || stringPlayerChoice == "P"){
            stringPlayerChoice = "Paper";
            success = true;
        } else if(stringPlayerChoice == "s" || stringPlayerChoice == "S"){
            stringPlayerChoice = "Scissors";
            success = true;
        } else {
            cout << "Invalid Choice." << endl;
            Sleep(500);
            cout << endl;
            cout << "Please only choose between Rock, Paper, Scissors." << endl;
            cout << "Type R for Rock." << endl;
            cout << "Type P for Paper." << endl;
            cout << "Type S for Scissors." << endl;
            Sleep(500);
            cout << "Enter your choice : ";
            cin >> stringPlayerChoice;
            cin.clear();
            fflush(stdin);
        }
    }while (!success);

    cout << "You has choosen " << stringPlayerChoice << "." << endl;
    Sleep(500);
    cout << "Loading result..." << endl;
    Sleep(3000);
    cout << "The bot has choosen ";
    Sleep(2000);
    cout << stringProgramChoice << endl;
    Sleep(1000);

    cout << endl;
    if (stringPlayerChoice == "Rock"){
        if (stringProgramChoice == "Rock"){
            cout << "Its a tie!" << endl;
            cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl << endl;
            Sleep(2000);
            cout << "======== Game Start ========" << endl << endl;
            rpsProgramAnswer(Balance, Cash, Amount);
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Paper"){
            Cash -= Amount;
            cout << "You Lose!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "A winner come from a losers who doesnt give up!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";            
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Scissors"){
            Cash += Amount;
            cout << "You Win!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "Dont stop until you are bored of moneys!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";
        }
    } else if (stringPlayerChoice == "Paper"){
        if (stringProgramChoice == "Rock"){
            Cash += Amount;
            cout << "You Win!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "Dont stop until you are bored of moneys!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Paper"){
            cout << "Its a tie!" << endl;
            cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl << endl;
            Sleep(2000);
            cout << "======== Game Start ========" << endl << endl;
            rpsProgramAnswer(Balance, Cash, Amount);
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Scissors"){
            Cash -= Amount;
            cout << "You Lose!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "A winner come from a losers who doesnt give up!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";  
        }
    } else if (stringPlayerChoice == "Scissors"){
        if (stringProgramChoice == "Rock"){
            Cash -= Amount;
            cout << "You Lose!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "A winner come from a losers who doesnt give up!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";  
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Paper"){
            Cash += Amount;
            cout << "You Win!" << endl;
            cout << "Because you are " << stringPlayerChoice << " and The Program choosen " << stringProgramChoice << "." << endl;
            cout << "Dont stop until you are bored of moneys!" << endl;
            cout << "Your Cash now is : $" << setprecision(2) << fixed  << Cash << ".";
        } else if (stringProgramChoice == "Scissors"){
            cout << "Its a tie!" << endl;
            cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl << endl;
            Sleep(2000);
            cout << "======== Game Start ========" << endl << endl;
            rpsProgramAnswer(Balance, Cash, Amount);
        }
    }

    Sleep(2000);
    cout << endl << endl;
    cout << "Wanna continue playing? (Y/N) : ";
    cin >> Choice;
    if (Choice == "Y" || Choice == "y"){
        cout << "Restarting the Game..." << endl;
        Sleep(2000);
        startRockPaperScissors(Balance, Cash);
    } else {
        casinoMenu(Balance, Cash);
    }
}

string rpsProgramChoiceToString(int ProgramChoice){
    string stringProgramChoice = " ";
    switch (ProgramChoice){
    case 1:
        stringProgramChoice = "Rock";
        break;
    case 2:
        stringProgramChoice = "Paper";
        break;
    case 3:
        stringProgramChoice = "Scissors";
        break;
    default:
        break;
    }

    return stringProgramChoice;
}

    cout << "=== Rock Paper Scissors ===" << endl << endl;
    cout << "A Game that will broke your fingers!"<< endl;

05/11/23, 10:32â€¯am - Ken: #include <iostream>
#include <string>
using namespace std;

int getDigit(const int number);
int sumOddDigits(const string cardNumber);
int sumEvenDigits(const string cardNumber);

int main(){
    string cardNumber; // String buat Credit card number
    int result; // Hasil total dari posisi angka ganjil dan genap

    cout << "Enter your Credit Card number : ";
    getline(cin, cardNumber);

    result = sumEvenDigits(cardNumber) + sumOddDigits(cardNumber); // Mentotal angka setelah di konfigurasi

    if (result % 10 == 0){ // Ngecek kalo nomer Credit Card bisa dibagi 10 atau tidak
        cout << cardNumber << " is valid!"; // Kalo bisa berarti valid
    } else {
        cout << cardNumber << " is not valid"; // Kalo gk bisa berarti gak valid
    }

    return 0;
}

int getDigit(const int number){
    // Misah angka yang dikali hasilnya ada 2 angka
    // Misal angka argument nya 12, asalnya dari 6 * 2
    // Karena angkanya 12 maka akan dipisah jadi 1 2
    // Dan kedua angka tersebut ditambah menjadi 3
    // Lalu di return angka 3

    return number % 10 + (number / 10 % 10);
}

int sumOddDigits(const string cardNumber){
    int sum = 0;

    for(int i = cardNumber.size() - 1; i >= 0; i-= 2){ // Ngambil setiap angka yang di posisi ganjil dari kanan ke kiri
        sum += cardNumber[i] - '0'; // Mengubah string ke int
    }

    return sum;
}

int sumEvenDigits(const string cardNumber){
    int sum = 0;

    for(int i = cardNumber.size() - 2; i >= 0; i-= 2){ // Ngambil setiap angka yang di posisi genap dari kanan ke kiri
        sum += getDigit((cardNumber[i] - '0') * 2); // Mengubah string ke int lalu dikali 2 dan di kirim ke getDigit function
    }

    return sum;
}

/*
 Luhn Algorithm
 --------------

 1. Pangkatkan setiap angka kedua dari kanan ke kiri. Kalo angka yang di pangkatkan hasilnya ada 2 digits, pisah jadi dua.
 2. Tambahkan semua angka yang ada pada step 1
 3. Ambil semua angka pertama dari kanan ke kiri lalu tambahkan semua
 4. Sum step kedua dan ketiga
 5. Kalau step 4 dapat dibagi 10, maka Credit Card adalah valid 
*/

26/11/23, 9:30â€¯am - Ken: #include <iostream>
#include <ctime>

#define winnerLoseCheck(x) spaces[x] == player ? std::cout << "YOU WIN!" : std::cout << "YOU LOSE!"
#define winnerBoardCheck(x, y, z) spaces[x] != ' ' && spaces[x] == spaces[y] && spaces[y] == spaces[z]

void drawBoard(char *spaces);
void playerMove(char *spaces, char player);
void computerMove(char *spaces, char computer);
bool checkWinner(char *spaces, char player, char computer);
bool checkTie(char *spaces);

int main() {
    char spaces[9] = {' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' '};
    char player = 'X';
    char computer = 'O';
    bool running = true;

    drawBoard(spaces);

    while(running){
        playerMove(spaces, player);
        drawBoard(spaces);
        if(checkWinner(spaces, player, computer)){
            running = false;
            break;
        } else if(checkTie(spaces)){
            running = false;
            break;
        }

        computerMove(spaces, computer);
        drawBoard(spaces);
        if(checkWinner(spaces, player, computer)){
            running = false;
            break;
        } else if(checkTie(spaces)){
            running = false;
            break;
        }
    }

    std::cout << '\n' << "Thanks for playing!";

    return 0;
}

void drawBoard(char *spaces){
    std::cout << '\n';
    std::cout << "     |     |     " << '\n';
    std::cout << "  " << spaces[0] << "  |  " << spaces[1] << "  |  " << spaces[2] << "   " << '\n';
    std::cout << "_____|_____|_____" << '\n';
    std::cout << "     |     |     " << '\n';
    std::cout << "  " << spaces[3] << "  |  " << spaces[4] << "  |  " << spaces[5] << "   " << '\n';
    std::cout << "_____|_____|_____" << '\n';
    std::cout << "     |     |     " << '\n';
    std::cout << "  " << spaces[6] << "  |  " << spaces[7] << "  |  " << spaces[8] << "   " << '\n';
    std::cout << "     |     |     " << '\n';
    std::cout << '\n';
}

void playerMove(char *spaces, char player){
    int number;

    do {
        std::cout << "Enter a number (1-9) : ";
        std::cin >> number;
        std::cin.clear();
        fflush(stdin);
        
        number--;
        if(spaces[number] == ' '){
            spaces[number] = player;
            break;
        }
    } while (!number > 0 || !number < 8);
}

void computerMove(char *spaces, char computer){
    int number;
    srand(time(0));
    std::cout << "Computer Move" << '\n';

    while(true){
        number = rand() % 9;
        if(spaces[number] == ' '){
            spaces[number] = computer;
            break;
        }
    }
}

bool checkWinner(char *spaces, char player, char computer){
    
    if (winnerBoardCheck(0, 1, 2)){
        winnerLoseCheck(0);
    } else if (winnerBoardCheck(3, 4, 5)){
        winnerLoseCheck(3);
    } else if (winnerBoardCheck(6, 7, 8)){
        winnerLoseCheck(6);

    }  else if (winnerBoardCheck(0, 3, 6)){
        winnerLoseCheck(0);
    }  else if (winnerBoardCheck(1, 4, 7)){
        winnerLoseCheck(1);
    }   else if (winnerBoardCheck(2, 5, 8)){
        winnerLoseCheck(2);

    }   else if (winnerBoardCheck(0, 4, 8)){
        winnerLoseCheck(0);
    }  else if (winnerBoardCheck(2, 4, 6)){
        winnerLoseCheck(2);
    } else {
        return false;
    }

    return true;
}

bool checkTie(char *spaces){

    for(int i=0; i < 9; i++){
        if(spaces[i] == ' '){
            return 0;
        }
    }

    std::cout << "ITS A TIE!" << '\n';
    return 1;
} <This message was edited>

27/11/23, 5:20â€¯pm - Ken: 1. In the Windows search bar, type Settings to open your Windows Settings.
2. Search for Edit environment variables for your account.
3. In your User variables, select the Path variable and then select Edit.
4. Select New and add the MinGW-w64 destination folder you recorded during the installation process to the list. If you used the default settings above, then this will be the path: C:\msys64\ucrt64\bin.
5. Select OK to save the updated PATH. You will need to reopen any console windows for the new PATH location to be available.

27/11/23, 5:36â€¯pm - Bagus Smp: #include <iostream>

using namespace std;

int main() {
	int bil1, bil2;
	
	cout<<"masukkan nilai x: ";
	cin >> bil1;
	
	cout<<"masukkan nilai y: ";
	cin >> bil2;
	
	//operator AND
	bool hasilopand = (bil1 > bil2) && (bil1 == bil2);
	
	//operator OR
	bool hasilopor = (bil1 !=bil2) || (bil1 > bil2);
	
	//operator negasi
	bool hasilopsi = !(bil1 > bil2);
	
	if (hasilopand) {
		cout << "operator AND = (x > y) && (x == y) = True " << endl;
	} else {
		cout << "operator AND = (x > y) && (x == y) = False " << endl;
	}
	if (hasilopor) {
		cout << "operator OR = (x !=y) || (x > y) = True " << endl;
	} else {
		cout << "operator OR = False = (x !=y) || (x > y)" << endl;
	}
	if (hasilopsi) {
		cout << "operator NEGASI = !(x > y) = True " << endl;
	} else {
		cout << "operator NEGASI = !(x > y) = False" << bil1 << endl;
	}
	
	return 0;
}

[28/11 14.18] VinixÂ¹: #include <iostream>
#include <climits>
#include <string>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    const int jumlahAnak = 5;
    const int jumlahNilai = 5;

    char nama[jumlahAnak][50];
    int nilai[jumlahAnak][jumlahNilai];

    for (int i = 0; i < jumlahAnak; ++i) {
        cout << "Masukkan nama anak " << i + 1 << ": ";
        cin >> nama[i];

        cout << "Masukkan nilai anak " << i + 1 << ": ";
        for (int j = 0; j < jumlahNilai; ++j) {
            cin >> nilai[i][j];
        }
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < jumlahAnak; ++i) {
        cout << "Anak " << nama[i] << " - Nilai: ";
        int totalNilai = 0;
        int minNilai = nilai[i][0];
        int maxNilai = nilai[i][0];

        for (int j = 0; j < jumlahNilai; ++j) {
            totalNilai += nilai[i][j];

            if (nilai[i][j] < minNilai) {
                minNilai = nilai[i][j];
            }

            if (nilai[i][j] > maxNilai) {
                maxNilai = nilai[i][j];
            }
        }

        double rataRata = static_cast<double>(totalNilai) / jumlahNilai;
        cout << "Total: " << totalNilai << ", Rata-rata: " << rataRata << ", Min: " << minNilai << ", Max: " << maxNilai << endl;
    }

    return 0;
}

		$('#dissmiss-alert').click(function(){
			$('.alert').addClass('hide');
		});

		$('#btn-login').click(function(){
			$('#username').attr('readonly', true);
			$('#password').attr('readonly', true);
			$('#btn-login').attr('disabled', true);

			$.ajax({
				dataType	: 'json',
				url 		: "content.php",
				data 		: {
					module		: 'exam',
					component	: 'auth',
					action		: 'process',
					proc		: 'login',
					user		: $('#username').val(),
					pass		: $('#password').val(),
				},
				success		: function(result){

					if(result.status == 'true'){
						window.location.href=result.link;
					}else{
						$('.alert').removeClass('hide');
						$('#text-error').html(result.error);

						$('#username').val('');
						$('#password').val('');
					}

					$('#username').attr('readonly', false);
					$('#password').attr('readonly', false);
					$('#btn-login').attr('disabled', false);
				},
				error 		: function(e){
					console.log(e);
				}
			});
		});
		</script>

30/01/24, 5:31â€¯pm - Bagus Smp: #include <iostream>
#include <climits>
#include <string>

using namespace std;
int main()	{
	
	const int banyaknilai = 7;
	string Namadepan, Namatengah, Namabelakang, absen, kelas, jurusan;
	int nilai[banyaknilai];
	
	cout << "Masukkan nama lengkap: ";
	cin >>  Namadepan >> Namatengah >> Namabelakang;
	string namasiswa = Namadepan + " " + Namatengah + " " + Namabelakang;

	cout << "Masukkan absen: ";
	cin >> absen;
	
	cout << "Masukkan Kelas: ";
	cin >> kelas >> jurusan;
	string kelassiswa = kelas + " " + jurusan;
	
	cout << "Masukkan nilai PTS: ";
	cin >> nilai[0];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai tugas 1: ";
	cin >> nilai[1];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai tugas 2: ";
	cin >> nilai[2];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai UH 1: ";
	cin >> nilai[3];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai UH 2: ";
	cin >> nilai[4];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai UH 3: ";
	cin >> nilai[5];
	cout << "Masukkan nilai PAS: ";
	cin >> nilai[6];

	int maxnilai = INT_MIN;
	int minnilai = INT_MAX;
	int totalnilai = 0;
	
	for (
		int i = 0; i < banyaknilai; ++i)
		{
		if (
			nilai[i] > maxnilai
			)
				{
				maxnilai = nilai[i];
				}
		if (
			nilai[i] < minnilai 
			)
				{
				minnilai = nilai[i];
				}
		totalnilai += nilai[i];
		}
		
		double rataRata = static_cast<double>( totalnilai ) / banyaknilai;
	
	cout << "\nHasil:\n";
	cout << "Nama: " << namasiswa << endl;
	cout << "Kelas: " << kelassiswa << endl;
	cout << "No. Absen: " << absen << endl;
	cout << "Nilai Maksimum: " << maxnilai << endl;
	cout << "Nilai Minimum: " << minnilai << endl;
	cout << "Rata-rata Nilai: " << rataRata << endl;
	
	return 0;
}

#define COLS 2

using namespace std;

int main()
{
    int tahun = 2010;
    int cell = 10;
    int penjualan[ROWS][COLS];

    for (int i = 0; i < ROWS; i++)
    {
    	cout << "\nPenjualan Tahun " << i+tahun;
    	cout << "\n--------------------\n";
    for (int j=0; j < COLS; j++)
    {
    	cout << "Data ke-" << j + i;
        cout << " = ";
        cin >> penjualan[i][j];
	}
	}
    cout << "Data penjualan pertahun\n";
    cout << "-----------------------\n";
    for (int i = 0; i < ROWS; i++)
    {
        cout << "\nTahun " << tahun + i;
        cout << "\n-----------------\n";
    for (int j = 0; i < COLS; i++)
    {
        cout << j + i << ") ";
        cout << penjualan[i][j] << endl;
    }
    }
    return 0;
}

#include <string>
using namespace std;

// Declare a structure named "car"
struct car {
  string brand;
  string model;
  int year;
};

int main() {
  // Create a car structure and store it in myCar1;
  car myCar1;
  myCar1.brand = "BMW";
  myCar1.model = "X5";
  myCar1.year = 1999;

  // Create another car structure and store it in myCar2;
  car myCar2;
  myCar2.brand = "Ford";
  myCar2.model = "Mustang";
  myCar2.year = 1969;
  
  // Create another car structure and store it in myCar3;
  car myCar3 = {"Nissan ", "GT-R ", 2017};
 
  // Print the structure members
  cout << myCar1.brand << " " << myCar1.model << " " << myCar1.year << "\n";
  cout << myCar2.brand << " " << myCar2.model << " " << myCar2.year << "\n";
  cout << myCar3;
  return 0;
}

  int z = x;
  x = y;
  y = z;
}

int main() {
  int firstNum = 10;
  int secondNum = 20;

  cout << "Before swap: " << "\n";
  cout << firstNum << secondNum << "\n";

  // Call the function, which will change the values of firstNum and secondNum
  swapNums(firstNum, secondNum);

  cout << "After swap: " << "\n";
  cout << firstNum << secondNum << "\n";

  return 0;
}

04/02/24, 6:05â€¯pm - Bagus Smp: #include <iostream>
#include <string>

using namespace std;

const int KURSI_MAKSIMAL = 80;

struct film {
    string judul;
    string waktutayang[8];
    int sisakursi;
    int hargatiket;
};

void app ()  {
    cout << "--------------  Dix ID  ---------------" << "\n\n\n";
    cout << "- Sedang Tayang" << "\n\n";
}

int main()  {
    film films[5];
    films[0] = {"ANCIKA: DIA YANG BERSAMAKU 1995",      {"08.00", "10.00", "12.00", "14.00", "16.00", "18.00", "20.00", "22.00"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 20000};
    films[1] = {"AGAK LAEN",                            {"08.00", "09.45", "11.30", "13.15", "15.00", "16.45", "18.30", "20.15"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 30000};
    films[2] = {"NYATANYA CUMA TEMAN",                  {"09.10", "10.30", "11.50", "13.10", "14.30", "15.50", "17.10", "18.30"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 25000};
    films[3] = {"DIA YANG  TAK MENCINTAI MU",           {"08.00", "09.50", "11.40", "13.30", "15.20", "17.10", "19.00", "20.50"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 40000};
    films[4] = {"The Quintessential Quintuplets Movie", {"08.30", "10.36", "12.42", "14.48", "16.54", "19.00", "21.06", "23.12"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 35000};

    int pilihfilm, pilihwaktu, jumlahtiket;
    char lanjut;

    do {
    app();

    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++)
    {
        cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[i].judul << "\n";
    }

    cout << "\nPilih Film (1-5): ";
    cin >> pilihfilm;
    
    if (pilihfilm >= 1 && pilihfilm <= 5)
    {
        pilihfilm--;

        cout << "\n Jam Tayang untuk " << films[pilihfilm].judul << ":\n";

        for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i)
        {
            cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[i] << "\n";
        }

        cout << "\nPilih Jam Tayang (1-8): ";
        cin >> pilihwaktu;

        if (pilihwaktu >= 1 && pilihwaktu <= 8)
        {
            pilihwaktu--;

            cout << "\nJumlah Tiket yang Dibeli: ";
            cin >> jumlahtiket;

            if (jumlahtiket > 0 && jumlahtiket <= films[pilihfilm].sisakursi)
            {
                films[pilihfilm].sisakursi -= jumlahtiket;

                int totalHarga = jumlahtiket * films[pilihfilm].hargatiket;

                cout << "\nPembelian Tiket Sukses!\n";
                cout << "Film: " << films[pilihfilm].judul << "\n";
                cout << "Jam Tayang: " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[pilihwaktu] << "\n";
                cout << "Total Harga: " << totalHarga << " Rupiah\n";
            }
            else {
                cout << "\nMaaf, jumlah tiket tidak valid atau kursi sudah penuh.\n";
            }
        }
        else {
            cout << "\nInput jam tayang tidak valid.\n";
        }
    }
    else {
        cout << "\nInput film tidak valid.\n";
    }

    cout << "\nIngin melakukan transaksi lagi? (y/n): ";
    cin >> lanjut;
    } 
    while (lanjut == 'y' || lanjut == 'Y');

    cout << "\nTerima kasih telah menggunakan layanan kami. Selamat menonton!\n";

    return 0;
}

const int KURSI_MAKSIMAL = 80;

struct film {

    int hargatiket;
   
};

void app() {
    cout << "--------------  DiG ID  ---------------" << "\n\n\n";

    int totalHarga[99];
    int hargaakhir;
    int x = 1;
int main() {
    film films[5];
    films[0] = {"ANCIKA: DIA YANG BERSAMAKU 1995", {"08.00", "10.00", "12.00", "14.00", "16.00", "18.00", "20.00", "22.00"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 20000};
    films[1] = {"AGAK LAEN", {"08.00", "09.45", "11.30", "13.15", "15.00", "16.45", "18.30", "20.15"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 30000};
    films[2] = {"NYATANYA CUMA TEMAN", {"09.10", "10.30", "11.50", "13.10", "14.30", "15.50", "17.10", "18.30"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 25000};
    films[3] = {"DIA YANG  TAK MENCINTAI MU", {"08.00", "09.50", "11.40", "13.30", "15.20", "17.10", "19.00", "20.50"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 40000};
    films[4] = {"The Quintessential Quintuplets Movie", {"08.30", "10.36", "12.42", "14.48", "16.54", "19.00", "21.06", "23.12"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 35000};

    int pilihfilm, pilihwaktu, jumlahtiket;
    char lanjut;

    do {
        app();

        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) 
        {
            cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[i].judul << "\n";
        }

        cout << "\nPilih Film (1-5): ";
        cin >> pilihfilm;

        while (pilihfilm < 1 || pilihfilm > 5)
        {
            cout << "\nInput film tidak valid. \nPilih Film (1-5): ";
            cin >> pilihfilm;
        }

        pilihfilm--;

        cout << "\n Jam Tayang untuk " << films[pilihfilm].judul << ":\n";

        for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
            cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[i] << "\n";
        }

        cout << "\nPilih Jam Tayang (1-8): ";
        cin >> pilihwaktu;

        while (pilihwaktu < 1 || pilihwaktu > 8) {
            cout << "\nInput jam tayang tidak valid. \nPilih Jam Tayang (1-8): ";
            cin >> pilihwaktu;
        }

        pilihwaktu--;

        cout << "\nJumlah Tiket yang Dibeli: ";
        cin >> jumlahtiket;

        while (jumlahtiket <= 0 || jumlahtiket > films[pilihfilm].sisakursi) {
            cout << "\nMaaf, jumlah tiket tidak valid atau kursi sudah penuh. \nUlangi input Jumlah Tiket yang Dibeli: ";
            cin >> jumlahtiket;
        }

        films[pilihfilm].sisakursi -= jumlahtiket;
 
        totalHarga[x]= jumlahtiket * films[pilihfilm].hargatiket;

        cout << "\nPembelian Tiket Sukses!\n";
        cout << "Film: " << films[pilihfilm].judul << "\n";
        cout << "Jam Tayang: " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[pilihwaktu] << "\n";
        cout << "Total Harga: " << totalHarga[x] << " Rupiah\n";

        cout << "\nIngin melakukan transaksi lagi? (y/n): ";
        cin >> lanjut;
        hargaakhir += totalHarga[x];
        x++;

#include <string>

using namespace std;

const int KURSI_MAKSIMAL = 300;

struct film {
    string judul;
    string waktutayang[8];
    int sisakursi;
    int hargatiket;
};

void app() {
    cout << "--------------  DiG ID  ---------------" << "\n\n\n";
    cout << "- Sedang Tayang" << "\n\n";
}
    
    int totalharga[99];
    int hargaakhir;
    int x = 1;

int main() {
    
    film films[5];
    films[0] = {"ANCIKA: DIA YANG BERSAMAKU 1995", {"08.00", "10.00", "12.00", "14.00", "16.00", "18.00", "20.00", "22.00"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 20000};
    films[1] = {"AGAK LAEN", {"08.00", "09.45", "11.30", "13.15", "15.00", "16.45", "18.30", "20.15"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 30000};
    films[2] = {"NYATANYA CUMA TEMAN", {"09.10", "10.30", "11.50", "13.10", "14.30", "15.50", "17.10", "18.30"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 25000};
    films[3] = {"DIA YANG  TAK MENCINTAI MU", {"08.00", "09.50", "11.40", "13.30", "15.20", "17.10", "19.00", "20.50"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 40000};
    films[4] = {"The Quintessential Quintuplets Movie", {"08.30", "10.36", "12.42", "14.48", "16.54", "19.00", "21.06", "23.12"}, KURSI_MAKSIMAL, 35000};

    int pilihfilm, pilihwaktu, jumlahtiket;
    char lanjut;

    do {
        app();

        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) 
        {
            cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[i].judul << "\n";
        }

        cout << "\nPilih Film (1-5): ";
        cin >> pilihfilm;

        while (pilihfilm < 1 || pilihfilm > 5)
        {
            cout << "\nInput film tidak valid. \nPilih Film (1-5): ";
            cin >> pilihfilm;
        }

        pilihfilm--;

        cout << "\n Jam Tayang untuk " << films[pilihfilm].judul << ":\n";

        for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
            cout << i + 1 << " - " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[i] << "\n";
        }

        cout << "\nPilih Jam Tayang (1-8): ";
        cin >> pilihwaktu;

        while (pilihwaktu < 1 || pilihwaktu > 8) {
            cout << "\nInput jam tayang tidak valid. \nPilih Jam Tayang (1-8): ";
            cin >> pilihwaktu;
        }

        pilihwaktu--;

        cout << "\nTiket yang tersedia: " << films[pilihfilm].sisakursi;
        cout << "\nJumlah Tiket yang Dibeli: ";
        cin >> jumlahtiket;

        while (jumlahtiket <= 0 || jumlahtiket > films[pilihfilm].sisakursi) 
        {
            cout << "\nMaaf, jumlah tiket tidak valid atau kursi sudah penuh. \nUlangi input Jumlah Tiket yang Dibeli: ";
            cin >> jumlahtiket;
        }

        films[pilihfilm].sisakursi -= jumlahtiket;
 
     totalharga[x]= jumlahtiket * films[pilihfilm].hargatiket;

        cout << "\nPembelian Tiket Sukses!\n";
        cout << "Film: " << films[pilihfilm].judul << "\n";
        cout << "Jam Tayang: " << films[pilihfilm].waktutayang[pilihwaktu] << "\n";
        cout << "Total Harga: " << totalharga[x] << " Rupiah\n";

        cout << "\nIngin melakukan transaksi lagi? (y/n): ";
        cin >> lanjut;
        hargaakhir += totalharga[x];
        x++;
    } while (lanjut == 'y' || lanjut == 'Y');

        cout << "total harga : " << hargaakhir;

    cout << "\nTerima kasih telah menggunakan layanan kami. Selamat menonton!\n";

    return 0;
}

05/07/24, 9:31â€¯pm - Ken: Backstory

Bagus Kun dan Ken bersekolah di Doktrin Kemampuan Elite, semua muridnya berisikan dengan murid-murid berbakat elite, Namun murid-murid wajib merahasiakan kemampuan mereka sendiri-sendiri.
Bagus Kun dan Ken berada di kelas yang sama, mereka berdua pendiam di kelas. Bagus kun selalu dikerumuni oleh cewek-cewek, dan semua orang iri kepada nya. Ken tidak peduli dengan hal cinta karena dia adalah MC.

Pada suatu saat Ken menangkap basah Bagus Kun yang sedang memakai kemampuan rahasianya yaitu Memanipulasi pikiran benda hidup.
Ia sedang memanipulasi seorang siswi untuk mencintainya. Bagus Kun menjadi panik dan rela melakukan apa saja demi menyembunyikan kemampuannya, Ken menerima permintaan tersebut.
Esoknya, Ken menyuruh Bagus Kun untuk memanipulasi pikiran Guru untuk memberikan kunci jawaban ujian pada minggu mendatang, dan Bagus kun berjanji akan melakukannya. Namun Guru tersebut tidak memberikan kunci jawaban ujian sesuai perintah Bagus Kun. Bagus kun pun heran, "Mengapa guru tersebut tidak menuruti perintah ku? Rasanya seperti ada seseorang yang mencegahku melakukan ini" tanya Bagus kun. Bagus Kun sangat panik karena jika ia tidak bisa memanipulasi Gurunya maka kemampuan rahasia nya akan tersebar. Sampai akhirnya Bagus Kun tidak berhasil memanipulasi Gurunya.

Esok harinya Bagus kun sengaja untuk bolos sekolah dikarenakan ia takut Ken akan menyebar kekuatannya terang-terangan. Saat pukul 9:00 AM tepatnya saat istirahat, didepan pintu rumah Bagus Kun ada seorang pengirim surat yang sedang mengetok pintu. Bagus kun pun keluar dan menerima surat tersebut. Surat tersebut bertuliskan "Hadiah untuk seseorang yang tidak dapat memenuhi perintah ku....Hormat Ken".
Saat itu Bagus kun langsung mengingat kejadian kemarin dan tidak berani untuk membuka isi surat tersebut. Lalu Bagus kun melihat sampul balik surat tersebut, dan betapa mengejutkannya terdapat tulisan lagi bertuliskan "Jangan ragu untuk membuka surat ini Bagus kun, jika kamu tidak membuka surat ini sampai besok aku akan melakukan hal yang lebih parah daripada yang kulakukan sekarang".
Bagus kun terkejut "Apa maksudnya melakukan hal yang lebih parah daripada sekarang?! Apa artinya ia melakukan sesuatu hari ini!?". Saking paniknya Bagus Kun buru-buru membuka surat tersebut. "Aku telah memberi tau seorang murid, sekelas denganmu, tentang kekuatanmu" itulah isi surat tersebut.
Bagus kun tidak dapat berpikir lagi, ia merasa dirinya sudah tamat.

06/07/24, 9:11â€¯am - Ken: import re

datePattern = r"\d{2}/\d{2}/\d{2}, \d{1,2}:\d{2}â€¯(?:am|pm) - "
namePattern = r"^[a-zA-Z]+: "
generatedMessagePattern = r"Messages and calls are end-to-end encrypted\. No one outside of this chat, not even WhatsApp, can read or listen to them\. Tap to learn more\." 
character = ['', '']

with open('WhatsApp Chat with Vinix.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    for line in f:
        line_contents = re.sub(datePattern, '', line)
        name_contents = re.match(namePattern, line_contents)

        if name_contents:
            name = name_contents.group(0)[:-2]
            message = line_contents[len(name_contents.group(0)):]

            if character[0] == '':
                character[0] = name

            elif character[0] != name and character[1] != name:
                character[1] = name

            print(name)
            print(message)

        else :
            message = line_contents
            if re.match(generatedMessagePattern, line_contents) == None:
                print(message)
                

            

print("Ada 2 orang yang sedang chat disini yaitu " + character[0] + " dan " + character[1])

lineCount = 0
timelinePattern = r"\d{2}/\d{2}/\d{2}, \d{1,2}:\d{2}â€¯(?:am|pm) - "
namePattern = r"^[a-zA-Z]+: "

character = ['', '']


with open('WhatsApp Chat with Vinix.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    for line in f:
        
        lineCount += 1

        if lineCount != 1:

            line_contents = re.match(timelinePattern, line)

            line_cleared = re.sub(timelinePattern,'' ,line)

            if line_contents:

                name_contents = re.match(namePattern, line_cleared)

                if name_contents:
                    name = name_contents.group(0)[:-2]
                    message = line_cleared[len(name_contents.group(0)):]

                    if character[0] == '':
                        character[0] = name

                    elif character[0] != name and character[1] == '':
                        character[1] = name

                    print(name)
                    print(message)

                else:
                    print("Error player name cant have special symbol.")
                    break

            else :

                print(line_cleared)


if character[0] != '' and character[1] != '':
    print("Ada 2 orang yang sedang chat disini yaitu " + character[0] + " dan " + character[1])

lineCount = 0
timelinePattern = r"\d{2}/\d{2}/\d{2} \d{1,2}.\d{2} - "
namePattern = r"^[a-zA-Z]+: "

character = ['', '']


with open('Chat WhatsApp dengan Ken.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    for line in f:
        
        lineCount += 1

        if lineCount != 1 and lineCount <= 50:

            line_contents = re.match(timelinePattern, line)

            line_cleared = re.sub(timelinePattern,'' ,line)

            if line_contents:

                name_contents = re.match(namePattern, line_cleared)

                if name_contents:
                    name = name_contents.group(0)[:-2]
                    message = line_cleared[len(name_contents.group(0)):]

                    if character[0] == '':
                        character[0] = name

                    elif character[0] != name and character[1] == '':
                        character[1] = name

                    print(name)
                    print(message)

                else:
                    print("Error nama tidak dapat menggunakan simbol spesial.")
                    break

            else :

                print(line_cleared)

        elif lineCount == 50:
            break


if character[0] != '' and character[1] != '':
    print("Ada 2 orang sedang chat disini yaitu " + character[0] + " dan " + character[1])
else:
    print("Error loading player") <This message was edited>

06/07/24, 9:25â€¯pm - Ken: using UnityEngine;
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;
using System.Collections;
using Unity.VisualScripting;
using System.Collections.Generic;

public class WhatsAppConverter : MonoBehaviour
{

    static public PlayerController playerController;
    static List<string> characterDatas = new List<string>();

    static string[] characterNames = new string[2];


    void Start(){
        playerController = GetComponent<PlayerController>();
    }

    public static void ReadFile(string FilePath){

        int lineCount = 0;
        string timelinePattern = @"\d{2}/\d{2}/\d{2}, \d{1,2}:\d{2}â€¯(?:am|pm) - ";
        string namePattern = @"^[a-zA-Z]+: ";
        string mediaMessage = @"^\<Media omitted\>";
        string editedMessage = @"\<This message was edited\>";

        Debug.Log(FilePath);

        try{
            using (StreamReader sr = new(FilePath)){
                string line;


                while ((line = sr.ReadLine()) != null && lineCount < 50){
                    lineCount++;

                    if (lineCount != 1 && lineCount <= 50){
                        string lineCleared = Regex.Replace(line, timelinePattern, "");

                        Match lineContents = Regex.Match(line, timelinePattern);

                        if (lineContents.Success){
                            Match nameContents = Regex.Match(lineCleared, namePattern);

                            if (nameContents.Success){
                                string name = nameContents.Groups[0].Value;
                                string message = lineCleared.Substring(nameContents.Length);

                                name = name.Remove(name.Length - 2);
                                name = name[..1].ToUpper() + name[1..];

                                if (characterNames[0] == null)
                                {
                                    characterNames[0] = name;
                                }
                                else if (characterNames[0] != name && (characterNames[1] == null))
                                {
                                    characterNames[1] = name;
                                }

                                Match messageContents = Regex.Match(message, mediaMessage);

                                message = Regex.Replace(message, editedMessage, "");
                                
                                if(!messageContents.Success){

                                    SaveData(name, message);
                                    
                                } else {
                                    lineCount -= 1;
                                }

                            } else{
                                Debug.Log("Error: Player name can't have special symbols.");
                                break;
                            }
                            
                        } else{
                            Debug.Log(lineCleared);
                            lineCount -= 1;
                        }

                    } else if (lineCount == 50) {
                        break;
                    }
                    
                }
            }

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(characterNames[0]) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(characterNames[1])){
                Debug.Log($"There are 2 players chatting here: {characterNames[0]} and {characterNames[1]}");
                SendCharacterData();
            }
            else{
                Debug.Log("Error loading players.");
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            Debug.Log($"Error reading file: {e.Message}");
        }

    }

    static void SendCharacterData(){
        playerController.SetCharacterName(characterNames);
        playerController.characterDatas = characterDatas;
        
    }


    static int charNum;
    static void SaveData(string name, string message){

        string data;

        if(characterNames[0] == name){
            charNum = 1;
        } else if(characterNames[1] == name){
            charNum = 2;
        }

        data = charNum.ToString() + message;

        characterDatas.Add(data);

    }
}
